 It is said that there are two Chaturthi in lunar month

 The Chaturthi of the Shukla Paksha after Amavasya is called Vinayaka Chaturthi

 It is said that all the sorrows of those who fast and remember Lord Ganesha on both these days are gone

 tippaniyan According to Hindu scriptures, the fasting of Vinayaka Chaturthi is observed by those who aspire for Riddhi-siddhi i
e
 wealth, knowledge, mastery, etc
, while Sankashti Chaturthi is done with the purpose of mitigating (eliminating) the obstacles of life
 manyata ke anusaar in donon tithiyon ko shraddhalu raat main chandramaa ke udai hone baad use doodh or jal se arghya dekar or phool, fal, mishtann aadi arpit kar ke hi apana upwas todate hai
 In this way Vinayaka Chaturthi and Sankashti Chaturthi are fasted every month, but Ganesh Chaturthi is observed only on the Chaturthi date of the month of Bhadas

 In this way Vinayaka Chaturthi and Sankashti Chaturthi are fasted every month, but Ganesh Chaturthi is observed only on the Chaturthi date of the month of Bhadas

 The comments hindu dharmagranthon ke anusaar vinayak chaturthi kaa vrath ve log rakhte hai, jo riddhi-siddhi yani dhan, vidya, nipunata aadi ke abhilaashi hote hai, jabaki sankashti chaturthi jivan kii baadhaon kaa shaman (samaapt) karne ke uddeshy se kiya jaataa he
 According to the belief, devotees on both these dates break their fast only after the moon rises in the night by offering it with milk and water and offering flowers, fruits, sweets etc
 is prakaar vinayak chaturthi or sankashti chaturthi kaa vrath to har maheene main hota he, lekin ganesh chaturthi keval bhadon ke maheene kii chaturthi tithi ko kehete hai
 According to Hindu scriptures, the fasting of Vinayaka Chaturthi is observed by those who aspire for Riddhi-siddhi i
e
 wealth, knowledge, mastery, etc
, while Sankashti Chaturthi is done with the purpose of mitigating (eliminating) the obstacles of life

 Last year, the Ministry of Defense launched a pilot project of frozen chicken supply in the five command of the army which was for one year but using the same decision incorrectly started supplying frozen chicken in the northern command's Ladakh and Kargil sectors
 aise mushkil ilaakon main frosen chiken supplai ke liye sena ne alag se maanak tay kiye hai jabaki uttari cmand ne haal hi main tamilnadu kii company suguna foods ke saath jo short turm qaraar kiya usamen niyamon ko taak par rakh diya gaya
 Northern Command called for tender supply from November 15 to December 14, but on the last day of submission of the tender, the remaining firms were told that the one-month tender had been canceled
 aise main suguna foods ko theka kaise mila iskaa jawaab kisi ke paas nahin he
 Suguna Foods has received a tender of Rs 117 per kg, while on the same terms, other suppliers to Western Command are supplying chicken at a rate of only Rs 96
 lihaaja is theke main sena ko kareeb 28 lakh rupayon kaa chuunaa laga
 Army officials investigate the company which is contracted, but Suguna Foods got permission to supply frozen chicken before the investigation
 suguna foods kii factory tamilnadu main he jise theka aise vakt mila jab karnataka main bird flu kii ashanka ke chalate kerala ne tamilnadu se chiken mangane par roak laga rakhi he
 Suguna Foods manufactures 100% halal chicken, while the army takes great precaution about religion and 80% jerk chicken is used

 It seems that everyone agrees that it is good that three Dalits were crushed by a tractor in Rajasthan
 acha hi hua ki madhyapradesh main dalit pariwaron ko kuen se pani nahin lene diya gaya
 The Dalit diva has shared a song by Ambedkar in Maharashtra whose dalit youth was killed on ringtone
 ye sabhi twitor handle ek duusare ko pholo karte hai
 Two thousand people do not follow by number, but the issue is raised here without any logging
 maine aath-das twitor handle hi dekhe hai or inamen se zyaadaatar 2009 se lekar 2012 ke bich ke bane hue hai
 Twitter is generally followed by large news media and people in film and media
 @community Media naam se bane handle ne apil kii he ki ve ambedkar periyar student cirkil ke handle ko pholo karen or unka samarthan karen
 On the handle of Ambedkar caravan, Dr
 Bhimrao Ambedkar's thoughts and statements are shared
 @community Media ko 1849 log pholo karte hai or iske 8000 se zyaada twit hai
 Even the Twitter handle of Chandrabhan Prasad, who wrote the Dalit diary in Pioneer since time, does not follow more than 2000 people
 jabaki chandrabhan angrezi se lekar hindi ke tamaam channelon par bataur visheshgy aate rahete hai
 He is a well-known name but it seems that the non-ethnic metropolitan nationalists of the Twitter world are less interested in him
 chandrabhan ne iaiti madras ke chaatro kaa samarthan kiya he
 Nationwide support draws for Ambedkar Periyar Students Circle

 co / yh3mxya39d - Community Media (@babasaheb_org) May 30, 2015 @community Media tweets Dr
 Ambedkar's speeches and thoughts
 ek twit main doctor ambedkar kaa wo mashhoor kathan twit kiya gaya he ki shruti or smriti par aadhaarit dharm ko nasht kar do
 Jyotiba Phule's historical book Ghulamgiri has also been reported for free download
 @dalitwomenfight, @dallitfreedom, @dalitcamera, @dalitrising, @dalit_revolt naam se kuch or handle mili
 The only handle named @dalityuvadal was found which tweets in Hindi
 ise bhi 400 log bhi pholo nahin karte hai
 Some may find their tweets provocative, but if you look carefully, then they hurt those questions fiercely, which has made the silence of the wider society quite deep
 madhya pradesh main ek dalit yuvak ko ghodi par chadhane ke liye helmet pahananaa padaa kyonki savarna jatiyon ko laga ki ye unka apmaan he
 If the society, which is worried about caste, finds an excess in these things, then immediately expresses its displeasure, but why should its silence on such incidents be understood that it does not oppose racist exploitation
 dalit yuva dal ke twit tikhe zarur hai lekin sadak par hinsak hone ke bajaae likhakar chuppi ko todane kaa prayaas bhi to he
 In a tweet, it is said that Dalit men are cowardly, only then people of Savarna society are raping Dalit daughters
 nishchit rup se internet jagat main maujuud dalit mahila adhikaar manch aisi baton kaa samarthan nahin karenge
 Fearing the cowardice of Dalit men means that the solution has been taken out in such a way that it will not happen if they are not cowardly
 zaahir he yah samasya kaa samaadhaan aisi lalakaaron se nahin nikalnaa he
 Several Twitter handles showed that Dalit women's organization activists are also taking up the exploitation of caste through their international network
 tippaniyan Whether or not Dalit thinkers and the organization's threat on Twitter can break the supremacy of the right wing present here, but their presence is telling that they are not going to remain silent without voicing their voice
 is ladaai ko kai log aarakshan samarthan or virodh kii dhaal se ladane lagate hai yaa iske naam par bachane lagate hai
 The issue of exploitation of Dalits is not just about reservation
 vaise yah jaanane main koi harz nahin ki dakshinpanthi takatein aarakshan ke alaava shoshan or daman ke in kisson par kya raay rakhti hai
 Ambedkar does not belong to anyone just by holding a rally in the name of Ambedkar on 14 April
 aaj na kal in sawaalon se takaraana hi hoga
 No public opinion can be modern or nationalist without solving these questions

 co / yh3mxya39d kisi ko inke twit bhadakaau lag sakate hai lekin aap dhyaan se dekhenge to ye un sawaalon par ugr tareeke se chot karte hai jinhen lekar vyapak samaaj kii chuppi kaaphi gahari ho chuki he
 In Madhya Pradesh, a Dalit youth had to wear a helmet to climb a mare because the upper castes felt it was an insult to him
 jaat-paat ko lekar chintit samaaj ko inaki baton main atirek lagata he to turant naaraazgi zaahir kar detaa he magar aisi ghatnaon par uski chuppi kyon na samajhi jaae ki wo jativaadee shoshan kaa virodh nahin karata he
 The tweets of Dalit Yuva Dal are sharp but instead of being violent on the street, there is an attempt to break the silence by writing
 ek twit main kaha he ki dalit purush kaayar hai tabhi savarna samaaj ke log dalit betiyon par balaatkaar kar rahe hai
 Certainly, the Dalit Women's Rights Forum in the internet will not support such things
 dalit purushon kii kaayarta ko lalkaarane kaa matlab he ki iskaa samaadhaan is baat main nikaal liya gaya he ki ve kaayar na hon to aisa nahin hoga
 Obviously, the solution to this problem is not to come out of such challenges
 kai twitor handle se pataa chalaa ki dalit mahila sanghathan kii kaaryakarta apane antarrashtriya network ke zariye bhi jaat-paat ke shoshan ko uthaa rahi hai
 The comments twitor par dalit chintakon or sanghathan kii dhamak yahaan maujuud dakshinpanthiyon ke varchasv ko tod paati he yaa nahin magar unki maujuudagi bataa rahi he ki ve apni aawaaj bina sunaae chup bhi nahin rahane vaale hai
 Many people start fighting this fight against the shield of reservation support and protest or in the name of it
 daliton ke shoshan kaa masalaa sirf aarakshan kaa nahin he
 However, there is no harm in knowing what right-wing forces hold opinions on these stories of exploitation and repression apart from reservation
 sirf 14 april ko ambedkar ke naam par raily kar dene se ambedkar kisi ke nahin ho jate hai
 Will have to deal with these questions today or tomorrow
 desh kaa koi bhi janamat in sawaalon ko hal kiye bina na to aadhunik ho saktaa he na rashtravaadi
